[out:xml][timeout:3600]; ( node(2516540263)['species:wikidata'='Q61105']['species:wikipedia'='de:Cedrus libani']; ); (._;>;); out meta qt;//['wikipedia wikidata mismatch - follow wikipedia redirect - for species prefixed tags']


wikipedia wikidata mismatch - follow wikipedia redirect - for name:etymology prefixed tags
name:etymology:wikidata and name:etymology:wikipedia tags link to a different objects, because name:etymology:wikipedia tag points to a redirect that should be followed
Q8743 vs (missing) article redirects from it:Thomas A. Edison to it:Thomas Edison

[out:xml][timeout:3600]; ( way(242615837)['name:etymology:wikidata'='Q8743']['name:etymology:wikipedia'='it:Thomas A. Edison']; ); (._;>;); out meta qt;//['wikipedia wikidata mismatch - follow wikipedia redirect - for name:etymology prefixed tags']
